## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start] --> B{Command Line Mode}
    B -->|build-weighted-generator| C[Build Weighted Generator]
    B -->|build-execution-algorithm| D[Build Execution Algorithm]
    B -->|add-execution-algorithm| E[Add Raw Execution Algorithm]
    B -->|list-algorithms| F[List Algorithms]
    B -->|set-algorithm| G[Set Algorithm for Model Type]
    B -->|show-algorithm| H[Show Algorithm]
    
    C --> C1[build_weighted_generator_dict]
    C1 --> C2[Validate Schema]
    C2 --> C3[model_db.add_algorithm]
    C3 --> Z[End]
    
    D --> D1[Get Generator Algorithm]
    D1 --> D2[weighted_generator_algorithm]
    D2 --> D3[Sort by Weight]
    D3 --> D4[compile_execution_algorithm]
    D4 --> D5[model_db.add_algorithm]
    D5 --> Z
    
    E --> E1[Parse JSON Steps]
    E1 --> E2[build_execution_algorithm_dict]
    E2 --> E3[model_db.add_algorithm]
    E3 --> Z
    
    F --> F1[model_db.get_all_algorithm]
    F1 --> F2[Display Algorithms]
    F2 --> Z
    
    G --> G1[Validate Algorithm Type]
    G1 --> G2[model_db.set_ml_algorithm]
    G2 --> Z
    
    H --> H1[model_db.get_algorithm]
    H1 --> H2[Display Algorithm]
    H2 --> Z
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant CLI
    participant ml_utils
    participant model_db
    participant validator
    
    CLI->>ml_utils: build_weighted_generator
    ml_utils->>ml_utils: build_weighted_generator_dict
    ml_utils->>validator: jsonschema.validate
    validator-->>ml_utils: validation result
    ml_utils->>model_db: add_algorithm
    model_db-->>ml_utils: algorithm_id
    ml_utils-->>CLI: algorithm_id
    
    CLI->>ml_utils: build_execution_algorithm
    ml_utils->>model_db: get_algorithm(generator_id)
    model_db-->>ml_utils: generator_algorithm
    ml_utils->>ml_utils: weighted_generator_algorithm
    ml_utils->>ml_utils: compile_execution_algorithm
    ml_utils->>validator: jsonschema.validate
    validator-->>ml_utils: validation result
    ml_utils->>model_db: add_algorithm(execution_algorithm)
    model_db-->>ml_utils: algorithm_id
    ml_utils-->>CLI: algorithm_id
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
graph LR
    A[Temporal Weight] --> C[weighted_generator_algorithm]
    B[Featureset Weight] --> C
    D[Temporal Windows] --> C
    E[Model Hierarchy] --> C
    
    C --> F[Generate Combinations]
    F --> G[Calculate Weighted Score]
    G --> H[Sort by Score]
    H --> I[Execution Algorithm List]
    
    I --> J[Feature Set 1]
    I --> K[Feature Set 2]
    I --> L[Feature Set N]
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Idle
    
    Idle --> BuildingWeightedGenerator : build-weighted-generator
    BuildingWeightedGenerator --> ValidatingSchema : validate
    ValidatingSchema --> SavingToDB : schema valid
    ValidatingSchema --> Error : schema invalid
    SavingToDB --> Idle : save complete
    
    Idle --> BuildingExecutionAlgorithm : build-execution-algorithm
    BuildingExecutionAlgorithm --> FetchingGenerator : get generator
    FetchingGenerator --> GeneratingCombinations : generator found
    FetchingGenerator --> Error : generator not found
    GeneratingCombinations --> SortingByWeight : combinations generated
    SortingByWeight --> CompilingAlgorithm : sorting complete
    CompilingAlgorithm --> ValidatingSchema
    
    Idle --> ManagingAlgorithms : list/set/show
    ManagingAlgorithms --> Idle : operation complete
    
    Error --> [*]
    Idle --> [*]
```
